Important Domestic Telegrams Two

Proposal to Reduce Taxes on Domestic Goods 9

Liu Zhi proposed a plan to reduce taxes on domestic goods to enrich the people's livelihood, stating: When investigating tax levies in our country, increasing current revenue is often the only purpose. There is often no deep consideration or long-term plan for the survival and development of industry and commerce. Although the income side is better when the tax amount is initially increased, after a while, merchants will hesitate and industries will close down, gradually leading to economic decline and difficulties for both the upper and lower classes. How can we expect the people to be rich and the country to be strong? It is important to know that if the country wants to increase tax revenue, it must first cultivate the tax source. If the tax source is abundant, the treasury will naturally be rich. The so-called "the people are rich, then the country is rich." The method of cultivation is to first reduce the burden on industry and commerce, so that the cost of domestic goods is low and easy to sell, which is sufficient to compete with foreign goods. The current regulations on machine-made goods stipulate that all machine-made foreign-style goods, when transported and sold domestically, are exempt from all other taxes and likin except for the export tax and inland tax collected by the first customs post. When they are transported and sold overseas, they are exempt from all taxes and likin. This kind of method not only reduces the cost of domestic industrial products, which is enough to resist foreign goods, but also can promote international trade. It cannot be said that it is not a good method for the government to protect industry and commerce. However, the industry and commerce in the inland provinces have always been immature. There are very few machine-made products, most of which are household handicrafts and agricultural products, which are not included in the preferential treatment of domestic goods. In addition, the years of war have made transportation difficult, the local areas are dilapidated, and the people are not living together. Those engaged in industry and commerce not only feel the lack of raw materials but also feel the stagnation of transportation. Furthermore, the heavy taxation increases the cost of goods and makes sales difficult. As a result, industry and commerce are declining day by day, and government revenue is also gradually decreasing. This is because the government only wants to increase tax revenue and does not consider whether merchants and the people have the ability to bear the burden, so the result is the opposite. Moreover, the government has clearly ordered the revitalization of industry and the promotion of domestic goods, which are unanimously agreed upon by the whole country as the primary plan to save the country. At this time when industry and commerce are budding, suddenly imposing heavy taxes is like heading north by driving the chariot south. It is proposed to appropriately reduce taxes on manufacturing goods and major agricultural products to show encouragement, so that although the tax amount is small, the quantity of goods will increase. Not only will the income not decrease, but it will certainly increase day by day. Its benefits to tax revenue are indeed not small.

Proposal to Implement the Allocation of Autonomous Funds 10

Liu Zhi proposed a plan to implement the allocation of autonomous funds in order to prepare for local autonomy, stating: Local autonomy is the primary task during the period of political tutelage and is also the foundation of constitutional government. It is extremely important. If we want autonomy to be completed as scheduled, it is impossible to proceed without determining the funds in advance. The Third National Congress of our Party did not have time to discuss the resolutions on various cases. Regarding the second item of the first clause of the political category, temporarily allocate a part of the field tax collected from each county to be used as the autonomous funds for each county. The percentage is determined by the provincial government based on local conditions. The resolution was issued by the Central Executive Committee to the National Government to order the provinces to comply with it. Furthermore, the Second Plenary Session of the Third Central Executive Committee resolved to complete the county autonomy case, with 19 years as the period for completing the county organization and the end of 23 years as the period for completing the county autonomy. In recent years, due to military influence, most provinces have not been able to implement it. Now that the period for completing the county organization has arrived, there are only four years left for completing the county autonomy. It is imperative to reaffirm the previous proposal and strictly order the provinces to comply with the above resolution and promptly allocate temporary and regular expenses for preparing for autonomy from the field tax of each county as special funds so that they can be carried out in stages in order to complete the work of political tutelage and establish the foundation of constitutional government.

Mo Dehui Protests to Karakhan 11

Regarding the matter of publishing remarks in a confusing manner, Nanjing diplomatic circles learned that Soviet Russian representative Karakhan sent a letter to our representative Mo Dehui at the Sino-Russian meeting, stating that when Karakhan met with Mo Dehui on the 6th of this month, Mo had expressed that he would resolve the issue of the Chinese Eastern Railway according to the Sino-Russian Agreement, the Fengtian Agreement, and the Bery Agreement. At the same time, Karakhan published the original letter before obtaining our consent. Mo has been ordered by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to lodge a serious protest with Ka on the 17th. The original text said: At 11:00 PM on the 10th of this month, I received letter No. 93. After reading the full text in detail, there is a statement in which your representative stated to me during the conversation on November 6 that the status of the Chinese Eastern Railway should be restored according to the Sino-Russian Fengtian Agreement by the Bery Record. There must be no doubt about this point, and there can be no doubt about it. At 12:00 PM that night, I telegraphed to postpone the announcement and repeatedly stated to your representative that during the conversation on the 6th, because your representative talked about the status of the Chinese Eastern Railway, my representative said that the status of the Eastern Railway could not be completely in line with the Sino-Russian Fengtian Agreement. Your representative then said that what my representative said was tantamount to declaring that there was no guarantee for maintaining the restored status of the Eastern Railway. My representative then said to your representative that it was not against the restored status of the Eastern Railway, but it could not be insisted on maintaining the wording without any change. What should be done within the scope of the Sino-Russian Fengtian Agreement should still be carried out. However, the quotation in the letter is inconsistent with the truth of the conversation, and it was quoted and published without consent. My representative has no choice but to lodge a serious protest. As for what is stated in the letter, the current status of the Eastern Railway has not been changed without the consent of both parties. Before the current method of the Eastern Railway is changed or the Eastern Railway is redeemed by China, neither party should freely change it through unilateral actions. My representative can now declare that the current status of the Eastern Railway, which does not violate the provisions of the Sino-Russian Fengtian Agreement, should not be changed by either party before the current method of the Eastern Railway is changed or the Eastern Railway is redeemed by China without the consent of both parties. Based on the sincerity of past consultations, my representative sincerely hopes that the Sino-Soviet meeting that has already opened will continue to convene as soon as possible so that the actual work of this meeting can be carried out quickly and successfully in order to live up to the Chinese government's goal of increasing the friendship between the two nations of China and the Soviet Union and consolidating the good-neighborly relations between the two countries. (Special telegram on the 18th)

Beiping-Suiyuan Railway Robbery Case 15

Beiping At 9:00 AM on the 17th, the Beiping-Suiyuan westbound train was surrounded by more than 700 well-armed bandits at Guancun Station, 65 li from Pingdiquan. All the luggage was searched and 34 passengers and 3 railway staff, including the station master, were taken away. The station's cash was also robbed. The area belongs to the jurisdiction of the Jin army. The railway bureau telegraphed the Jin army to send the Eighth Cavalry Division to pursue them. On the 18th, 3 railway staff were released by the bandits, but one passenger was not released. Fortunately, there were no foreigners. The railway bureau has rushed to send the chief of the police department, Liang Hu, and Ding Wenqi to investigate the truth. Yu Xuezhong will postpone his trip to the Beiping-Hankou line due to the occurrence of this incident. There are many deserters and bandits in Chahar, and the Jin army is not serious about maintaining law and order and transportation. The Northeast Army will implement the advancement to the west of Tianzhen to take over the defense of the entire Beiping-Suiyuan Railway. Chairman Li Peiji has no power. Yan sent Zhao Chengshou to serve as the garrison commander. Guo Fengshan, the division commander originally stationed in Suiyuan, has fled. It is said that his subordinates, regiment commanders Mai Youchuan and Chen Yujia, were detained by Zhao and have been killed. The former provincial party committee member Ji Yifan and Chen Guoying were also arrested, and their life and death are unknown. Suiyuan has entered a world of terror. (Special telegram on the 18th)

Beiping Yu Xuezhong arrived in Beiping from Zhangjiakou at 6:00 PM today. (Special telegram on the 18th)

Beiping The passenger and freight mixed train that departed from the Xizhimen Station of the Beiping-Suiyuan Railway in Beiping yesterday morning was suddenly attacked by a large group of bandits at Hancun Station between Datong and Suiyuan this morning. There were about 700 cavalrymen in total. The entire train was robbed. The passengers were left with only their underwear, and more than 40 station staff and male and female passengers were taken away and fled west. This is the largest train robbery since the Lincheng incident in previous years. (Telegram on the 17th)

Discussion on Reducing Administration on the Chinese Eastern Railway 17

Harbin On the 18th, the Board of Directors of the Chinese Eastern Railway held a meeting on personnel reduction and administrative reduction. Russia advocated reducing 17 offices of the railway bureau and 2,000 Chinese and Russian personnel, including 600 full-time staff. China advocated reducing 600 staff without moving full-time staff. The two sides debated fiercely. As a result, a small group was first formed to review the case. On the 18th, the Chinese directors of the railway bureau held a meeting and resolved to oppose the reduction of 2,000 personnel. It was suggested that the revenue of the Chinese Eastern Railway was decreasing day by day, with an average daily income of 120,000 rubles and an average daily expenditure of 200,000 rubles, resulting in increasing losses. The Chinese Eastern Railway borrowed 3 million from the bank in the past and signed 2 million with the Chinese Bank on the 17th and 1 million with the Russian Far East Bank. The direct wireless telegraph test from Harbin to Kucha was successful and will be launched next month. (Special telegram on the 18th)

Opposition to Further Rent Collection in Jiangxi 29

Nanjing, 17th. After a joint petition by ten representative delegations from various Jiangxi hometown associations in Nanjing, a joint meeting was held. It was decided to telegraph Lu Diping, opposing further rent collection in Nanchang. The telegram stated: "The economy of the provincial capital is declining, and the vitality is almost exhausted. Recently, we heard about further borrowing, borrowing three months of business rent and one and a half months of housing rent. An investigation reveals that two months of shop rent had already been borrowed in early October, and the burden is already at its limit. How can one keep picking the melons under Huangtai? We earnestly hope that you will consider the plight of the surviving people and cancel this decision. The people of Jiangxi will be most grateful." A joint petition was made by representative delegations of Jiangxi associations in Beijing, Shanghai, Hankou, Hunan, Xiang, and Yue. (Special telegram on the 18th)

Foreign News

Second Session of the Indian Round Table Conference Held 51

Six-person presidium elected. Discussions ban eavesdropping. Indian representatives advocate for equal status, arguing that racial prejudice should no longer exist. Reuters, London, 17th. The second plenary session of the Indian Round Table Conference was opened today by British Prime Minister MacDonald, who delivered a speech urging the representatives to cooperate with each other and achieve success. The conference has decided to appoint MacDonald as chairman and Lord Sankey as vice-chairman, and to elect six people from the British representatives, Indian royal representatives, and British Indian representatives to form the presidium. It was also decided that news reporters would not be allowed to eavesdrop on the discussions, but the organizing committee would handle the release of news through the secretariat.

Reuters, London, 17th. The six people elected by the plenary session of the Indian Round Table Conference to serve on the presidium of the committee were British representatives Lord Reading and Lord Peel, Indian royal representatives Prince Bikaner and Prince Bhopal, and British Indian representatives Aga Khan and Sastri. During today's plenary session, British Indian representative Sapru (one of those who traveled between India and Gandhi to mediate between the two sides) rose to speak, outlining the changes that had taken place in India over the past ten years and the seriousness of the non-violent resistance movement, saying that the so-called parliamentary sovereignty was nothing more than the sovereignty of a few people in Britain and a few people in India. Therefore, Indians naturally demanded freedom as an integral part of the British Empire. Ordinary people often asked what the slogan of "dominion status" commonly used by Indians meant, but they did not know whether these ordinary Englishmen had used these words to Canada in 1865, or to Australia in 1900, or to South Africa in 1909. India was determined to obtain equal status with other dominions. The Indian government must be responsible to the Legislative Council. He hoped that the Indian royal family would move forward with the idea of ​​a unified India. The various parts of India would manage their own affairs and be absolutely independent within their own borders, but would be subject to appropriate relationship adjustments with others. The real major issue in India today, in the opinion of the Indians, was the All-India Federation. In the past 25 years, the Indian Minister's mishandling of the continuous mass movements had caused a great mistake. As for the commercial level, the Indians did not want to seize the capital of the Europeans, and the Indians were willing to welcome any suggestions from the Europeans to protect their rights. The issue of national defense was indeed difficult, but the Indians only asked for the opportunity to train their own troops. The British army could be under the control of the Indian Governor, and the Indians could raise funds to pay for the military expenditure. If it was said that British officers were unwilling to serve under the command of the Indians, this was a big mistake. It must be known that the idea of ​​superior and inferior races should not exist, otherwise India would never be convinced. (Applause) Indian royal representative Prince Bikaner rose to speak, first declaring the loyalty of the Indian royal family to the British Emperor, and then said that the Indian royal states must be influenced by the development of political thought and external systems. However, India was a place with different situations. If a complete country was to be established and a sovereign parliament was to be placed in Delhi, which would make all the major and minor events of the people of India decided by this, it would be impossible. This kind of constitution would not leave any room for the Indian royal states, and this kind of government would be overwhelmed by its own weight. Therefore, he advocated the use of a federal system to combine the Indian royal states with British India, while the rights of the princes arising from the treaty must be more clearly defined. Any disputes concerning treaty rights should be tried by a superior court. British Indian representative Jayakar described the views of Indian youth and said that if India was allowed to enjoy dominion status today, the call for independence would naturally disappear within a few months.

Reuters, London, 17th. A report from the Indian government on the situation in India during the week ending November 15 stated that the Round Table Conference currently being held in London was now highly regarded by the Indian people, and had shifted public attention to the conservative clauses used to resolve constitutional issues.

Reuters, Ahmedabad, 18th. Yesterday, 25 people were arrested here, including Sara Bab, the chairman of the Gujarat Provincial Congress, and the wife of a wealthy manufacturer.

Forty-Eight Banks Closed in the United States 52

Public uneasy. Associated Press, New York, 17th. According to today's news, several banks across the country have closed their doors one after another. Six banks in Lewis Town, Kentucky, two in Illinois, four in Missouri, one in Iowa, and thirty-five in Arkansas. The closure of these thirty-five banks was mostly due to public unease, as the difficulties in the banking sector in Connery had affected neighboring states. Several of these banks have been subject to runs, and some have used the law to suspend business for five days when subject to runs, in order to protect the interests of depositors. They may reopen within these days. At a time when the market is sluggish and unemployment is rampant, this banking crisis cannot be taken lightly.

Polish Parliamentary Elections 53

Government Party Wins Big. Reuters, Warsaw, 17th. The results of the Polish parliamentary elections are favorable to the government party led by General Pilsudski. The parliament has a total of 444 seats, and the government party alone has won 245 seats, thus gaining an absolute majority. The previous parliament was repeatedly in conflict because there was no absolute majority party. The main political program of the government party is to amend the constitution in order to increase the power of the president and the government.

The streets of the capital are now as quiet as a ghost town, with only a few policemen patrolling back and forth. Recent Thesis by the Italian Prime Minister 57

National Press Agency, London, 18th. The Daily Express today published an article by Mussolini, the full text of which concerned the future of peace in Europe and the reasons for its current unrest. It stated that many people were dissatisfied with the Treaty of Versailles and were unanimously demanding that the treaty be amended as soon as possible. He strongly advocated for universal disarmament. Although the European countries did not stop their military preparations for one day, Italy would not abandon its arms race. What person among us does not hope for the realization of peace, but we cannot therefore sit idle and abandon national defense in order to protect the integrity of our territory. May Heaven send punishment on anyone who invades the borders of Italy. If Italy is forced to enter a war, it will do its utmost to defeat the enemy.

Domestic News

Eighth Route Army Actively Prepares to Attack Yongning 65

Simultaneously Carrying Out the Pacification of Zhang Gui's Remnant Troops. Guangzhou Correspondence: The Battle of Nanning has been fluctuating between tense and relaxed for days. In terms of the situation, it has become tense again in recent days. The Eighth Route Army Headquarters hired a total of 320 small steamships in Wuzhou starting from the 7th. On the same day, it hired 12 electric boats and about 30 lighters in Guangzhou, which sailed to Wuzhou on the 8th. At present, it is estimated that there are more than 30 shallow-water steamships distributed to the Guiping area and more than 50 to the Guixian area. The Department of a certain brigade stationed in Zhaoqing has reportedly opened Wuzhou in order to transfer the 63rd Division stationed between Tengmeng to the left wing for reconnaissance. According to recent reports, the remnant enemy Zhang Gui's army has suddenly shifted its focus to Nanning and seems to be abandoning Liushu. Li Zongren's troops have moved and fled to Zhujiang, Bai Chongxi's troops have moved to Shanglin and Wuming, and Zhang Fakui's troops, Xue Yue, Huang Heling, and other troops are stationed in the east of Nanning City. In summary, the enemy seems to be focusing on the Yongchun and Hengxian areas from three routes. Therefore, the Eighth Route Army has also increased the transfer of the entire 63rd Division, Li Yangjing, to Guixian, and the 126th Brigade, Huang Zhiwen, has already opened to the front line of Guixian. The 125th Brigade, Huang Yanzhen, is also continuing to be transferred. Division Commander Li Yangjing, together with 125th Brigade Commander Huang Yanzhen and more than ten attendants and orderlies, took the Zhixin ship to Guixian on the evening of the 7th to supervise the attack on Yongning, and agreed with the 10th Route Army, Lu Han, to return to Pingma and attack Yongning together. The air force team was also deployed to cooperate in bombing the enemy with fierce bombs at that time. All the planes that set off to attack Yongning were temporarily handed over to Captain Hu Jinya for command. In this overall voice, there are also simultaneous rumors of pacifying the enemy army. It is said that with regard to Zhang Fakui's army, the former commander of the 12th Division of Zhang's army, Mr. Miao, was appointed as the general chief of staff of the headquarters. After Miao was appointed, he took office at the Eighth Route Army Camp in Wuzhou on the 8th. Regarding the recent collection of the Guizhou army, Ma Xiaojun has also been active. Ma was an old figure in the Guizhou army. In March of this year, he was once entrusted by the Central Government to carry out the pacification of the Guizhou army. At that time, the war in the north was intensifying, and the Guizhou army had no intention of surrendering. Now that Yan and Feng have fallen, it is difficult for the Guizhou army to survive for a long time, so Ma was again ordered to recruit. After Ma arrived in Wuzhou, he sent his former subordinate, Mr. Wei from Rong County (a relative of Wei Yunsong of the Guizhou army), to Nanning to negotiate everything first, and then reported it to the Central Government after the negotiations were completed. A telegram was sent by Ma to the generals of the Guizhou army, advising them to disarm, saying that the authorities could agree to give them a title to go abroad for two years and then allow them to return to the country and be given priority use. The following is a transcript of Ma's telegram: (Nanning deeply sends greetings to brothers Bai Jiansheng, Li Delin, and Huang Jikuan. After Feng and Yan's defeat, the Central Plains have been settled. The situation in Guizhou should be peaceful. If the brothers are willing to disarm and go abroad, the Central Government can organize a study tour and give each of them 50,000 yuan for travel expenses. After two years of returning to the country, they will be given priority use and their previous merits will not be forgotten. As for the reorganization of the troops and the proper handling of the aftermath, there are appropriate measures to be taken in person. At this point in time, it is time to stop. Prolonged fighting is useless and only harmful. Even if the brothers are willing to starve to death in the Western Mountains, they should also think of the descendants of Zhou Li. I have come today to seek mediation. If you agree, please telegraph to the Central Government for approval, or if you need to come in person to discuss, it is possible. How will the blessings and misfortunes be transferred in one thought? I hope for a quick reply. Ma Xiaojun bows) (November 11)

Troop Movements of the Joint Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi Bandit Suppression Forces 66

Hankou Dispatch: Since the Wuhan Military Headquarters issued an order on the 1st of this month for Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces to simultaneously suppress bandit communists, the mobilization of various bandit suppression troops by land and water has been vigorous. It is reported that the troops transferred back from the front include Xia Douyin's 13th Division, Zhi Zhi's 44th Division, Xu Yuanquan's 48th Division, Jiang Guangnai's 61st Division, Cai Tingkai's 60th Division, Chen Cheng's 11th Division, and the brigades of Liu Peixu, Rong Jingfang, and Xu Dezhao. Commander Xia's troops arrived first and stationed part of their force in Huangpi and Xiaogan in northern Hubei, responsible for guarding the southern section of the Pinghan Railway, while another part proceeded to eastern Hubei. The three divisions of Xu, Jiang, and Cai arrived successively, with Xu's division temporarily stationed in Wuhan and Jiang's and Cai's divisions heading to Hunan to then transfer to Jiangxi. Commander Chen's division has already arrived, with a part of Xiao's division moving last. It is reported that Xu's and Xiao's divisions and Liu's and Xu's brigades were originally under the command of Xu Yuanquan, the 16th Route Army Commander, with the area west of Hubei designated as their garrison area. Except for Xiao's division, which will be concentrated in Luoyang and move south today (the 17th), the remaining troops have completely arrived in Hankou. Yesterday, the 144th Brigade of Xu's division was ordered to proceed to Jingzhou and Shashi, and Liu Peixu's brigade also continued to set out today. It is expected that they will be fully deployed within three days. Xu's division will be stationed in Yichang, Shi'en, and Hefeng, Liu's brigade in Jianli, Xu's brigade in Xiantao, and Rong's brigade in Yuekou. Upon arrival, Xiao's division will be stationed in Shashi. As for Cai's and Jiang's divisions, they were ordered to proceed from Hunan to Jiangxi. Cai's division has already concentrated in Pingxiang, while Jiang's division is currently stationed in Miluo and Changsha. The 19th Route Army Headquarters remaining in Hankou will be led by acting Commander Guo Siyan to Hunan today, and the 8th Brigade will also set out on the same day. Brigade Commander Dai Ji will lead the 9th Brigade and the division headquarters to depart tomorrow. The transportation of this route army has now been completed. Chen Cheng's 11th Division was originally stationed in the Xinyang area, but due to a lack of vehicles, it could not be deployed as scheduled. Now that the southern section of the Pinghan Railway is fully open, it began moving south yesterday. Its first batch has already arrived in Hankou. The special service battalion, artillery battalion, and the military law and military supply departments have also arrived. The 33rd Brigade will continue to advance, with the 31st Brigade moving last. After arriving in Hankou, the division will station the 33rd Brigade in Qiaokou, the 33rd Brigade in Liujiamiao, and the 31st Brigade in Yuezhou, responsible for guarding the Wuchang-Changsha Railway line. (November 17th)

Progress of Bandit Suppression in Hubei Province 67

Hankou Dispatch: Bandit communists in Hubei Province have always been rampant, but still less so than in Hunan and Jiangxi provinces. Therefore, the authorities' bandit suppression plan prioritized Jiangxi, then Hunan, and finally Hubei. Recently, the two groups of He Long and Kuang Jixun attempted to attack Jinshi and Fengxian but failed, and then turned to attack Gongan, Shishou, Jianli, and other counties in southern Hubei, which were successively captured. At the same time, red bandits in northern Hubei also gathered in the northern countryside of Huangpi, echoing the bandits in southern Hubei from afar. The military situation of bandit suppression in Hubei Province had to become tense. Currently, the bandit communists in Huangpi have been defeated by Xia Douyin's and Xu Yuanquan's forces. The authorities have also dispatched a large army to search and suppress the bandits in southern Hubei. It is expected that they can be eliminated in about ten days. The situation of bandit suppression on each route is described separately below:

In Northern Hubei: Huangpi in northern Hubei is the thoroughfare of the Pinghan Railway. Although bandit communists are often found, there are at most only over a thousand. They are quickly pacified after the garrison troops rush to suppress them. On the 15th of this month, suddenly about ten thousand communist bandits surrounded Yaojiaji in the northern countryside of the county. The 75th Regiment of the 13th Division was originally stationed there. Because of the large number of bandits, they relied on the terrain and held fast. The bandits launched a brave assault, and the fighting was fierce. The regiment used machine guns to sweep them, and they retreated slightly, but the encirclement remained. After the regiment telegraphed Hankou for help, the Military Headquarters immediately ordered the 48th Division to dispatch two regiments to provide assistance and ordered Xu Yuanquan, Commander of the 16th Route Army, to personally command. After receiving the order, Xu led the replenishment regiments one and two of that division to rush there overnight. Xu personally supervised the battle, and the besieged troops of the 13th Division launched a pincer attack from inside and outside, finally defeating the bandit troops. Xu returned to Hankou on the 16th, while replenishment regiments one and two remained there temporarily to cooperate with the troops of the 13th Division to eliminate the remaining bandits. The bandit communists in Guanghua and other places are also very rampant and have been defeated by Fan Shisheng's troops of the 51st Division, fleeing into Henan Province.

In Southern Hubei: Honghu in southern Hubei has always been a communist stronghold. The pseudo-Hubei Provincial Party Department and the Soviet government are located there, and He Long, Kuang Jixun, Yun Daiying, and others are in charge. After repeated pursuits and suppressions by officers and soldiers, they have not been eliminated. Recently, He's bandits entered Hunan and attacked Jinshi and Fengxian but failed, and then turned back to southern Hubei, successively capturing Shishou, Jianli, and Gongan counties, and their momentum is very strong. In order to thoroughly resolve the bandit communists in that area, the authorities have drafted a plan and designated Xu Yuanquan's 48th Division, a part of Xiao Zhichu's 44th Division, a part of the 3rd Training Division, and the three brigades of Liu Peixu, Rong Jingfang, and Xu Dezhao to surround and suppress them, with Xu Yuanquan in charge of the command. Currently, a part of Xu's division has moved to Shashi, Liu Peixu's brigade has moved to Jianli, Xu Dezhao's brigade has moved to Xiantao, and Rong Jingfang's brigade has moved to Yuekou, forming a large encirclement towards Honghu. Xu's headquarters will be located in Shashi to facilitate command. Xu himself will personally supervise the suppression after each unit has fully arrived at the designated location. In addition, the bandit disaster in eastern Hubei is most serious in Huangmei, Guangji, Qichun, and other counties. Currently, the troops of the 13th Division are suppressing them, and most of the bandit troops have fled to the border of Anhui and Jiangxi. If no major forces join them, they should be able to be eliminated within ten days. (November 17th)

He Jian's Resignation Not Approved 68

Changsha Dispatch: He Jian, Chairman of the Provincial Government and Commander of the 4th Route Army, has been under heavy attack by people inside and outside Hunan. In addition, the bandit situation is rampant, and military salaries are exhausted. The environment is difficult to cope with. Therefore, on the 10th of this month, he telegraphed the central government, strongly resigning from all his positions. After the telegram was sent, it was kept strictly confidential, fearing that military morale would be shaken once the news spread. On the 13th, he received a reply telegram from Chairman Chiang, expressing warm words of consolation and retention, and then the telegram was made public. It is recorded as follows:

He Jian's Telegram of Resignation: I, your subordinate, was ordered to be in charge of Hunan's administration and to command the military affairs of the Fourth Route Army, as well as to handle the suppression of bandits, while also being responsible for guiding the party affairs of Hunan Province. Since taking office, I have been diligent day and night, fearing that I would not be up to the heavy responsibilities and that my efforts to govern would be ineffective, failing to live up to the great trust placed in me. Fortunately, I have followed your strategies in all matters and have worked hard to carry them out without any obstacles. Unexpectedly, within a few months, incidents have occurred one after another, with the Gui rebels and communist bandits successively fleeing to the provincial capital. I was filled with shame and anger. Although I relied on your virtue and power to recover quickly, I deeply regret that I was unable to eliminate the threat beforehand. I intend to resign immediately to give way to more capable people. At this time, the central government is using troops in Henan and Shandong, and the communist bandits have gathered in Pingxiang and Liuyang. Zhu Mao and Peng Huang, under the orders of the Third International, have united the mob and are trying their best to invade Hunan, attempting to advance into Wuhan and seize the political power of five provinces to implement a total national rebellion plan. Moreover, the remnants of the Gui and Zhang rebels are still entrenched in the area of Qiyang, Lingling, Dong'an, and Wugang, and the bandit atmosphere is rampant. The situation is tense, and I dare not rashly push aside my responsibilities, lest I be taken advantage of by the rebels and cause harm to the overall situation. I had to telegraph for instructions and continue to perform my duties, trying my best to remedy the situation. Now that Yan and Feng have been resolved, and Gui and Zhang are about to be destroyed, although the communist bandits are still active in the border areas of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi provinces, the central government has decided on an encirclement and suppression plan, and it will not be difficult to quickly pacify them. Military affairs are gradually coming to an end, and construction is urgently needed. I have always admired your knowledge and have served my hometown for many years, bearing heavy responsibilities. I am grateful for your kindness and will wholeheartedly devote myself to serving, not shying away from difficulties and dangers, and striving to repay you. However, my talent and wisdom are short, and I am not familiar with the opportunity to handle difficult Hunan issues. I have been laboring in vain and have not benefited the people. I have exhausted my strength and have not benefited the country. I have not made any contributions in the past, and I am even more fearful of walking on thin ice in the future. Therefore, I sincerely plead that I may be allowed to resign from all my positions and that someone be appointed to replace me immediately so that I may have the leisure to retire and devote myself to learning. In the future, I will serve the party and the country for a longer period of time. If I have any wisdom, I will still try to contribute it at any time. I respectfully submit this telegram and pray that you will examine it and give instructions to follow. Your subordinate, He Jian, kowtows.

Chairman Chiang's Reply Telegram to Changsha Commander He Yunqiao: I have received your telegram with respect. The suppression of communist bandits and the pacification of the region rely on your leadership. I urge you not to entertain the idea of resigning, so as not to disappoint the Central Government’s high expectations. Chiang Kai-shek’s official seal.

Jinan Telephone Company Appeal Case 69

The Part Regarding Provisional Execution Has Been Heard. Jinan Dispatch: In the case of the debt between the Jinan Telephone Company and the Japanese Dongtuo Corporation, the Jinan Local Court previously ruled that the Telephone Company should repay Dongtuo 1.2 million yuan and ordered provisional execution. The Telephone Company appealed to the High Court to revoke the provisional execution, while the other party asked the Local Court to extend the provisional execution for one month. The court ruled that the provisional execution be extended for 20 days from November 1st. If the Telephone Company could not fulfill its debt obligation by the deadline, the provisional execution would be enforced. After the appeal of the provisional execution, the Shandong High Court scheduled a hearing for today (the 15th). The lawyer for the appellee, the Dongtuo Corporation, Japanese national Yoshida, requested a temporary leave, which was rejected by the court. The hearing began at 2:00 PM today. Because the provisional execution had already been ruled, it could only be canceled by a judgment. Therefore, a collegiate panel was formed. Those who appeared in court were the Presiding Judge of the High Court, Gan Jianshu, Judge Yi Xinding, Judge Yikui, and the agent lawyer of the Telephone Company, Yan Chenghan and Jia Rongqing. The court first asked the appellant for the reasons for requesting the revocation of the provisional execution, and Yan Chenghan argued according to law. The court also asked about the business situation of the Telephone Company. Yan replied that in the 14th year of the Republic, there were only 2,100 telephone lines in the city, and now it has increased to 2,615. The court then announced the end of the debate and scheduled the judgment for the 17th.

Procedures for Collecting Business Registration Fees in Jiangsu Province 70

The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Finance issued the procedures for collecting business registration fees in various counties yesterday. They are recorded as follows: (1) The regulations and detailed rules for collecting business registration fees have been passed by the Provincial Government Committee and should be implemented by the directors of the county finance bureaus and the county magistrates, who should supervise the collection directors. (2) Business registration should be implemented from January of the 20th year of the Republic, and two months should be spent on preparatory investigation and reporting procedures. (3) Business registration certificates will be printed and issued by the department to the county bureaus for requisition. (4) Plaques will be issued by the department. The style will be issued by the department, and the county bureaus will manufacture and number them according to the style. (5) The report forms for each store mentioned in Article 4 of the regulations will be issued by the department. The style will be issued by the department, and the county bureaus will make and issue them separately for filling out and filing for future reference. (6) The fee vouchers and fine receipts mentioned in Article 7 of the implementing rules will be printed and issued by the department for future use. (7) The number of staff members mentioned in Article 10 of the implementing rules should be determined according to the size of the county and employed according to the expense table and reported for record. (8) The chairman of the county chamber of commerce mentioned in Article 12 of the implementing rules should be hired as a consultant by each county, and their names should be reported for record. (9) The investigation roster mentioned in Article 13 of the implementing rules will be issued by the department. The county bureaus will follow the style to complete the investigation and submit it for verification. (10) The fee of two jiao for each plaque mentioned in Article 2 of the regulations will be retained by the county bureau for the purpose of making and issuing plaques and printing report forms and investigation rosters. (11) The fee of two jiao for each business registration certificate mentioned in Article 10 of the regulations should be remitted to this department for the purpose of printing registration certificates, etc.

Local News

Songjiang 72

Funding for People's Organizations: The county's party and government conversation meeting yesterday discussed the issue of funding for people's organizations. The county party department proposed to approve the finance bureau's reply that there were no funds available for allocation to people's organizations other than those included in the budget. Regarding how to raise funds to benefit people's movement, the conversation resulted in a decision to grant a total of 450 yuan in subsidies to people's organizations that are organized or reorganized for three months. This amount should be allocated from the original 807 yuan in funds for this item throughout the year, excluding the funds for the Agricultural Consolidation Association. As for the 200 yuan per month newly stipulated for the Agricultural Consolidation Association, the original 13 yuan and 45 cents should be used to offset it, leaving a shortfall of over 100 yuan. Furthermore, when other people's organizations are organized and established in the future, the source of their recurring expenses should be jointly submitted by the county government to the provincial department for approval and replied to the county party department.

New Public Security Bureau Chief Takes Office on a Fixed Date: Zhu Ying, the director of the County Public Security Bureau, was promoted by the provincial government to director of the Huaiyin Public Security Bureau. Shen Jing, director of the Qiushan Public Security Bureau, has been transferred to Songjiang. The county government has forwarded the order to notify him. Director Shen has specially sent the chief of the Luodian sub-bureau and inspectors to Songjiang to discuss everything related to the takeover. It is heard that Director Shen is scheduled to take office in Songjiang on the 25th.

Provincial Organization Minister Inspects Party Affairs: Huang Yuren, the organization minister of the Provincial Party Department, came to Songjiang on the 15th to inspect the work of reorganizing party affairs in the county. The reorganization committees of the County Party Department reported on their recent work, and Huang added instructions. After the inspection, he left Songjiang on the same day and returned to Shanghai.

Joint Defense Meeting of Three Counties Continues: The joint defense office of the three counties of Songjiang, Jinshan, and Shanghai was previously established. Yesterday (the 17th), another joint defense meeting was held in this county. The magistrate of Shanghai County, Yan Shenyu, and the magistrate of Jinshan County sent a district chief as a representative to Songjiang. The meeting was held in the afternoon to discuss the meeting. After the meeting, the county magistrate of Jinshan hosted a night banquet. Magistrate Yan and others took a night express train back to Shanghai.

Suzhou 73

Unemployed Youth Commits Suicide in Suzhou: A man from Wuxi named Yu Henian checked into the First Hostel outside of Gate the day before yesterday (the 17th). Yu was working in the Shanghai Nanhua Printing Bureau. Recently, he lost his job and had no face to return home. After arriving at the hostel, he suddenly had a pessimistic thought. He bought a bottle of sedative pills outside. Yesterday morning at about 10:00 AM, the waiter at the hostel saw that Yu was still in bed and opened the door to enter. He saw that Yu was lying on the bed with a miserable expression, knowing that he had taken poison. He searched the room and found two suicide notes, one to his parents and one to the hostel. The hostel and the waiter immediately reported the incident and hired a car to send Yu Henian to Suyong Hospital for treatment. Dr. Gu gave him emergency treatment. Fortunately, the poisoning was mild, and his life was saved. The hostel sent a letter to his father, Hui Zhong, to come to Suzhou to take care of him. His father came to Suzhou after hearing the news. There was a lot of regret in his suicide note that he should not have been absurd that day.

Ward Chief Accused by Detainees: Zhou Jiyun and other detainees at the Third Ward of Sifang Street jointly submitted a report to the Ministry of Justice last month accusing Ward Chief Lei and Gao Dongheng, the chief of the Second Section, of corruption, rebellion, and extortion, requesting a thorough investigation. Minister Zhu instructed the chief prosecutor of the High Court to investigate and verify the matter in detail yesterday (the 18th).

Suspicious Regiment Commander to be Sent to Capital for Verification: The 4th Gendarmerie Regiment captured Xu Jingzhi, the owner of the Xuyuantai Silk Factory, on Jingde Road the day before yesterday and found an appointment letter for the commander of the Xu Huaihai Guerrilla Regiment of the Anti-Rebel Army, many blank appointment forms, and correspondence between the secretary Jiang Weihua and Deng. According to Xu, the title of regiment commander was obtained by spending 500 yuan. Therefore, the Gendarmerie Regiment Commander Jiang has decided to escort Xu and the other two to the Capital Garrison Headquarters for verification within a few days.

Kunshan 74

Investigating the Sauce Dispute: Anting Town, a county under the jurisdiction of Kunshan County, borders Jiading and is known for its commercial activities. The border between Kunshan and Jiading has been the source of repeated disputes since the establishment of the salt checkpoints last year. Last night, a small shipment of sauce transported by a Jiading boat was spotted by a checkpoint guard and was detained. When the ship crew refused, they were beaten. Bystanders were outraged and gathered to question the guards at the checkpoint. It was late at night, and the noise alarmed the residents. Fortunately, Yang Jiwei, the commander of the town's defense corps, ordered his men to gather and, along with Magistrate Ma and others in the town government, worked hard to mediate, and the matter was peacefully resolved.

Wuxi 75

Complaint Filed Over Fare Increase on Xicheng Bus Line: Since the Xicheng long-distance bus line started operating, business has been good, but the road surface is rugged and dangerous, and the bus travels dangerously. Recently, Hua Meixuan and other citizens of the Fifth District (Tianshang City), Yanqiao Town, filed a complaint with the Construction Department, accusing the company of illegally increasing the fare (the original fare from Wuxi to Yanqiao was 2 jiao, but it has recently been changed to 3 jiao), endangering passengers, and damaging provincial roads, requesting that personnel be sent to secretly investigate and order the county to order a halt to operations. Yesterday, a reply was received, stating that the company's original fare was indeed low, and that it had requested a change due to excessive losses, which was approved by the Department after review and had not exceeded the standard. The request to order the county to halt operations should not be considered.

Four-County Joint Defense District Holds Meeting in Wuxi: The Director of the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province, Hu Pu'an, issued a special order to the magistrates of various counties to organize joint defense because communist bandits in Jiangsu Province have been rampant for years and have not been suppressed. The province was divided into sixteen joint defense districts. This county, Jiangyin, Wujin, and Changshu were one joint defense district, with Magistrate Pan as the director of the joint defense district. After receiving the order, Magistrate Pan specially scheduled the first joint defense meeting of the four counties of Xichang, Chengwu, and Changshu at the county administration storage on the 18th to discuss defense methods and sent a letter to the three counties of Chengchang and Wu in advance to prepare proposals and attend the meeting on schedule. Yesterday (the 18th), the magistrate of Jiangyin County, Li Leng, representative Li Zonggang (chief of the county public security bureau), the magistrate of Changshu County, Tan Jijue, the magistrate of Wujin County, Wu Deyao, and the second district chief of the provincial public security team stationed in Xishui, Mao Mujun, and four other people attended the meeting at 2 pm. The following resolutions were reached: (1) The second meeting will be held on the 29th of this month. (2) Magistrate Pan will draft the budget for the joint defense office and the detailed rules for handling affairs. (3) The joint defense office will be located in Wuxi. (4) The establishment of each county will be set for December 1st. The magistrates of each county returned to their original counties on the same day.

Punishment for Abusing Grandmother: Cheng Aju, a villager in Zhouxin Town, Yangming Township, under the jurisdiction of this county, is naturally fierce and does all kinds of evil. His grandmother, Cheng Wu, is over seventy years old and takes care of her own meals and chores day and night. A few days ago, Cheng Aju complained that his grandmother was slow, so he loudly scolded and slapped her several times, causing her face and gums to become bruised and swollen, and she was in extreme pain and fell to the ground. Afterwards, Cheng Wu reported to the 8th Branch of the Public Security Bureau, which had jurisdiction. The chief of the branch, Wang Chongxi, immediately sent police officers to arrest Cheng Aju. After Wang conducted a preliminary examination, the case was deemed to involve defiance and impiety, so he prepared a document yesterday and sent it to the Public Security Bureau for legal action.

Changshu 76

Chinese Medicine Doctor Kidnapped and Ransom Demanded: Zhang Chengqi, a Chinese medicine doctor in Xiyang Town, Fushan District, and Zhang Baoqi, a farmer, were robbed by pirates and kidnapped along with several children on the 5th of this month. After receiving the letter, the Zhang family is making every effort to raise the money.

Yangzhou 79

Husband Killed By Wife And Her Lover: In Chenjiawei, Balipu, in the second district of the county, Chen Hengqi, who worked as a barber, married Wang five years ago. Not long after, he went to Japan to continue his barbering career and did not return for many years. His wife then had an affair with Sun Rongchen from Zou. When Chen suddenly returned home on the eighth day of the seventh lunar month of this year, Sun was concerned that future interactions would be difficult. So he became determined to kill him. Chen had a headache a few days ago, and Sun visited him, saying that he had a very effective medicine for headaches at home that he could try. After saying this, he sent a bottle of medicine. Chen, because Sun was a neighbor for many years, did not suspect him and took it. Unexpectedly, he died within a few hours. Afterwards, Chen's uncle Jin Ren believed that the cause of death was unclear, and reported the incident to the 2nd Branch of the Public Security Bureau. The police were dispatched to arrest Wang, but Sun had already fled upon hearing the news. Yesterday, the branch escorted Wang to the court, where the prosecutor's office interrogated her once. According to her confession, she had been having an affair with Sun for four years, but she has not yet admitted to the murder. This morning (the 17th), the prosecutor Lu Kaisheng of the court, accompanied by an forensic official, went to investigate.

Human Trafficker Escorted To Court: A farmer in Dinggou Town in this county, Song Youpeng, reported to the 7th Branch of the Public Security Bureau that his wife had been seduced and trafficked by Yin Wanshan in the vicinity. The police were immediately dispatched to arrest Yin. Yesterday (the 16th), he was escorted to court for investigation and handling according to the law.

Qia Long's Bankruptcy and Shen Yu's Closure: After Qia Long Bank in Yangzhou went bankrupt, Shen Yu Bank on Brick Street also announced its closure on the 15th. It is reported that the reason was the suspicion of Manager Mei Jun, and the rumors spread, causing the other banks in the city to rush to withdraw money, making it difficult to circulate. Yesterday (the 16th), the Money Industry Association calculated that the number of debts was not large. It is heard that Bian Yanghui will return to Yangzhou to handle the matter and can be reorganized after some cleaning. It is also known that after the collapse of Qia Long Zhuang, the association calculated that it owed 70,000 taels in deposits, tens of thousands of taels in public singles in this street, 60,000 taels to five or six peers in Zhenjiang, 20,000 taels to Shen Zhuang, 3,000 taels in capital, tens of thousands of taels in dividends over the years, 20,000 yuan in underreported debts, 6-7,000 taels in Daji, and 100,000 taels to shops and hometown households in Shanghai Fuzhou. Yesterday (the 16th), the first branch of the Public Security Bureau ordered the second branch office to arrest shareholder Bian Da. After arriving at the Public Security Bureau, he was temporarily released on bail for cleaning. According to the industry, the store can recover about 60 to 70% of the debts and deposits.

Pinghu 80

Robbery Occurs At Huxiao Bridge: At around 10:00 PM on the night before last (the 25th), more than twenty bandits with more than ten fast guns and the rest wielding long and short wooden sticks suddenly arrived at Xiebang, three miles northeast of Huxiao Bridge Town, broke into the homes of Lu Lanrong and Lu Wenrong, and robbed the local villagers. Huzhou 81

Bandits Revenge on Villagers: Changxing, Xia Yuan Ferry, South Tang Li Area. Villager Shen Shunliu was a former Qing Dynasty student, over sixty years old, and his family was destitute. His son, Amao, farmed for a living. However, Shen Shunliu was often careless in his speech and easily aroused resentment. Some time ago, bandits such as Xu Changsheng were hiding in that area, and after the resident Mei Security Team soldiers surrounded and captured many of them, the escaped bandits were wanted. The bandits believed that Shen had been the one who revealed their presence, so at about eleven o'clock the night before last, seven or eight bandits, each carrying a handgun, suddenly arrived at his home, broke down the door, and shot Shen Shunliu in his bed. He was shot in the chest and died instantly. Afterwards, the bandits left, leaving a letter claiming revenge.

Lao Da: Ding Wang Jingqi; Central Da: Inviting Chu Minyi; Tsinghua: Students Propose Three Candidates

Nanjing, 18th: The Ministry of Education stated that the presidents of the three national universities, Central University, Labor University, and Tsinghua University, will be announced on time within a week. Meiji University Student Riot 85

Students Detained, School Suspended. Tokyo, 18th: According to a telegram, after a student assembly at Meiji University at 10:20 this morning, more than two thousand students stormed the faculty room, shouting angrily and throwing chairs, tiles, and stones, destroying window glass, furniture, and other items, engaging in a chaotic brawl with faculty and staff. To prevent any eventuality, two hundred police officers arrived and were stationed outside the school. Seeing the situation deteriorate, they entered the school to suppress the students. The students' enthusiasm reached its peak, making it difficult to subdue them. The executive committee declared that they would learn from the Soviet system in order to achieve their goals. However, the attitude of the students supported by the general affairs committee and the sports department is noteworthy. The school authorities have announced a temporary suspension of classes.

Japan's United Press, Tokyo, 18th: The turmoil at Meiji University, which has been continuously unresolved, reached its peak today. It was learned today that a student assembly resolved to strike the entire school tomorrow. At the same time, student riots occurred everywhere in the school, destroying glass windows, chairs, and other items. The school authorities requested the police station to dispatch two hundred patrol officers to the school to suppress the students. Several students were detained.

Ministry of Education Issues Senior High School Commercial Course Curriculum 86

Yesterday, the Ministry of Education issued an order to the education departments and bureaus of various provinces and cities regarding the temporary standards for the senior high school commercial course curriculum. The original order stated: "The temporary standards for various courses in kindergartens, primary schools, junior high schools, and senior high school general studies, as formulated by the Ministry, have already been issued. Now, the temporary standards for the senior high school commercial course curriculum have also been printed. In addition to distributing them separately, we are sending two copies of this order for your department to forward to the senior high school commercial schools under your jurisdiction. If there are insufficient copies, please purchase them directly from bookstores selling these standards. Please also instruct the schools under your jurisdiction to conduct practical experiments accordingly and submit the results of the experiments and research to the Ministry for review."

Explanation of the Temporary Standards for Senior High School Commercial Courses: The curriculum standards were compiled by the drafting committee for the senior high school commercial course curriculum of the Ministry of Education, printed and distributed by the Zhonghua Book Company, priced at 30 cents. The explanation of the book is described in five points as follows: (1) The process before the formulation of this standard is mostly similar to the temporary standards for kindergarten, primary school, junior high school, and senior high school general studies curricula, which have been detailed in the beginning of the compilation of primary and secondary school curriculum standards and the explanations of various established curriculum temporary standards. However, this standard relies more on the efforts of various experts, so it was not finalized and sent to print until August of the nineteenth year. (2) The drafting of this standard first formulated a general table as a basis for the drafting of each subject, but the general table also underwent multiple revisions. After the drafting of each subject was completed, it was revised once as a whole (the general table is detailed in the original book). (3) The Party Ideology course can use the same standard as the general studies course and should be formulated by the Central Party Headquarters. Military training and world geography also use the same standards as the general studies course. Military training has separate regulations, and world geography is detailed in the temporary standards for the general studies course. The subjects in the general elective course can adopt the standards of each subject in the general studies course and increase or decrease the content according to the credits. Therefore, the curriculum standards for Party Ideology, military training, and general elective courses are not included in this standard. (4) The drafting, sorting, and review personnel of this standard are now listed as follows: Wang Zuliang, Li Quanshi, Zhang Yisun, Zu Rui, Pan Wen'an, Sun Saibing, He Bingsong, Li Peien, Zhao Shifu, Pan Xulun, Tang Yan, Yuan Cao Boquan, Zheng Hesheng, Tang Qingzeng, He Dekui, Ma Yinchu, Cai Zhengya, Chen Tingrui, Shi Boxing, Qiu Zhenglun, Zhang Deyi, Wu Wenwei, Yan Xie, Yang Rumei, Wu Dongchu, Yang Yinpu, Wang Shizhen, Wang Yingbin, Yang Xingfo. In addition, Gu Shusen, Dai Yingguan, and Chen Zhe from the Ministry of Education, Zhu Jingnong, Zhao Naichuan, and Wu Yan from the Standing Committee of the General Assembly, as well as the various committee departments attending the General Assembly, participated separately. (5) Why is the trial period of this standard limited to one year, and will it be revised in detail in the future? During the trial period, we hope that those who conduct practical experiments will report the results of the experiments and research to this committee for reference.

Zhejiang Affiliated Primary School Joint Conference Standing Committee 87

Twenty-one Representatives Registered; More Than Thirty Important Cases Resolved: The third session of the Zhejiang Affiliated Primary School Joint Conference was held in Jiande on November 12. Attendees included Zhu Wenzhi and Zhao Yuren from the Education Department, Xu Yunhui and Cheng Shizhen from the Senior High School Affiliated Primary School, Li Yongzhang and Shen from the Second High School Affiliated Primary School, Jiang Xien and Wu Yungong from the Third High School Affiliated Primary School, Gui Zuan and Jin Yisun from the Fourth High School Affiliated Primary School, Ying Huaide and Tian Xi'an from the Fifth High School Affiliated Primary School, Wu Zhenxi from the Sixth High School Affiliated Primary School, Li Mianshao and He Yu from the Seventh High School Affiliated Primary School, Jin Yue and Zhou Tingluo from the Eighth High School Affiliated Primary School, Wang Chongyu and Xi Pincheng from the Ninth High School Affiliated Primary School, Jin Xian from the Tenth High School Affiliated Primary School, and Mo Ruxiao from the Eleventh High School Affiliated Primary School. The opening ceremony was held at 1:00 PM on the afternoon of the 12th at the Jiande County General Chamber of Commerce. Wang Chongyu, the representative from the Fifth Primary School of the General Affairs Department, chaired the meeting. Representatives from the County Party Headquarters, Director Dong of the Jiande Education Bureau, and the Education General Representative from the Tenth Primary School spoke successively. The first meeting was held from 7:00 PM to 9:00 PM that evening, still chaired by Representative Wang. A general assembly was held on the morning of the 13th, and Representative Jin of the Tenth Primary School was elected as chairman. A welcome party was held at 9:00 PM by the Ninth Primary School, and all representatives attended. Representatives Zhao from the Education Department, Jin from the Tenth Primary School, and Xu from the Senior High School gave speeches. The students of the Ninth Primary School performed various excellent items. The party ended happily at 10:00 PM. On the morning of the 14th, a general assembly was held again. At 11:00 AM, the Jiande Education Bureau, the Public Education Center, and the First and Second Primary Schools jointly held a welcome party. Representatives Zhao from the Education Department, Jin from the Tenth Primary School, Li from the Second Primary School, and Zhou from the Eighth Primary School proposed improvements to local education and discussed them in detail. The closing meeting was held in the afternoon. There were more than thirty resolutions passed at this conference, the more important of which were: drafting a method for assessing the academic performance of primary school students, editing the Zhejiang Primary School Education Journal, continuing to test the Ministry-issued temporary standards for the primary school curriculum, assigning tasks to test the urgent problems to be solved in local primary schools, stipulating that the next research problem should focus on academic performance assessment, collecting teaching aids and drawings made by each primary school, and submitting them to the Education Department for submission to the Ministry of Education to compile primary school music textbooks. It was also decided that the fourth regular meeting would be held in Wuxing, and at the same time, a performance assessment method and a teaching aid exhibition would be held.

Statistics on the Number of University Students in Zhejiang Province 88

The Zhejiang Education Department compiled a total of 530 students based on the replies from eight schools. The Zhejiang Education Department had previously prepared a survey form to investigate the number of university students from the province and sent it to domestic universities to fill out. The following is a list of the seven schools that have already reported: (1) National Central University: 161 (144 males, 17 females); (2) National Sun Yat-sen University: 17 (15 males, 2 females); (3) National Labor University: 87 (84 males, 3 females); (4) National Tongji University: 32 (30 males, 2 females); (5) Shanghai Private Fudan University: 191 (170 males, 21 females); (6) Shanghai Private Datong University: 30 (26 males, 4 females); (7) Henan Sun Yat-sen University: 5 (4 males, 1 female); (8) Peking Union Medical College Hospital: 7 (4 males, 3 females). A total of 530 people (477 males, 53 females). The rest are awaiting investigation and statistics.

Local News

Tongwen Chinese Students Strike 92

The Tongwen College in Xujiahui, Shanghai, which was established by the Japanese, also enrolls Chinese students and is divided into two departments: the main department and the Chinese department. Few people pay attention to it. Recently, due to excessive oppression of the Chinese department, a strike has been triggered. The details are as follows:

Initially, the Republican Daily published an article about the corruption of Tongwen College. The school authorities suspected that Wang Zhaogan and Guo Qimeng, two first-year students of the department, were responsible. Suddenly, on November 8, they received a notice from the school summoning them for a conversation, forcing them to withdraw from the school, and filling out the withdrawal application and stamping it on their behalf. The students were very angry when they heard about it. The student union raised questions and asked the school to announce the reasons for the expulsion and their crimes. The school authorities replied that there was no need to announce the reasons, and showed the withdrawal application filled out on behalf of the two students, saying that it was not an expulsion. After repeated negotiations, they were asked to withdraw the order. The school authorities knew that they were at a disadvantage and their means were despicable, so they tried to find a declaration of the Academic Research Association commemorating the October Revolution and falsely accused the two students of issuing it. The student union said that the school arbitrarily took a declaration from an off-campus organization, which was not enough to prove that the two students' actions were detrimental to the personal future of the two students, and asked the school to provide evidence. The school authorities refused strongly, saying (the school's decision to expel has been made, whether or not it was done by these two students, the student union has no right to interfere). Japanese imperialism is so contemptuous of Chinese students, which is also an insult to the Chinese nation. The student union could no longer tolerate it, so it convened a general meeting of all students last night (the 17th) and decided to strike together on the 18th and put forward seven conditions, demanding a satisfactory response from the school authorities, vowing not to resume classes until victory. The Japanese students in the headquarters also protested against the school's improper handling of the matter and took the same action as the Chinese students, with the right to initiate a strike.

Declaration of All Students of the Labor and Agricultural College 94

National Labor University Agricultural College All Students Declaration on Su Rugan, Fang Cheng, etc. Accusation of Students:

If the personality of all the youth of a college is innocently accused, even if one has the power to cover the sky with one hand, where will the justice of the world exist? Even if justice is unfortunately lost, if public opinion is still there, it is difficult to conceal the injustice of our generation. The facts are presented to the people of our country. Since the turmoil in our school, we have already issued a declaration for criticism from people of all walks of life. Recently, Su Rugan, Fang Cheng, and others have falsely accused all the actions of the students in their letter to President Li, saying that they were all instructed by President Li personally. It should be known that the opposition of the students to the school affairs meeting and the expulsion of Chen, Fang, Wu, and Jin are our own initiative. The second declaration on November 11 can be used as a reference. The content of the letter, except for matters related to the president's personal affairs, does not ask, but there are many that involve our character and insult the actions of the students, such as (All those in the student declaration should also be fully available in the letter, which is tantamount to confessing that the master of this student unrest is Mr. himself), etc., as if (the declaration) cannot be consistent with (the letter), and the opinions must be different from the president. If the facts coincide, the inside story will be revealed. What kind of bizarre method of proof has ever been found after searching the logic? How can it be reasonable to erase the truth? The declaration of our people has its own fair attitude, and the (letter) of the president has its own claims. How can they be confused? It was found that the declaration of students of the Workers' and Peasants' Colleges on October 31 opposed Li Lianggong as the president. Today, the letter from Mr. Su Fang and others to the president also expressed this attitude without prior consultation. If this is used to accuse the gentlemen of being our running dogs, even if the words are as good as Su Fang's, etc., how will they answer? Furthermore, the expulsion of Chen from the Horticulture Department and the expulsion of Fang Wu from the Agronomy and Chemistry Department are also indiscriminately and forcibly referred to as Li's instigation. Alas, the light of a word, where does the personality of the youth of a dignified university exist? It is also a good job to trap people in injustice. Things must rot before insects are born. The three gentlemen Chen, Fang, and Wu do not reflect on their own faults, but shamelessly use indiscriminate words to confuse the hearing and make people feel ashamed, then the expelled should have no place to stand. If the world has truth, then the absurd people should have something to wake up with. Here are the details (1) The expulsion of Chen from the Horticulture Department was due to the student's own initiative. The second declaration has already detailed it. And Chen then secretly fought with Zhang Nong, the director of the farm, for whether or not the horticultural area was independent in the management of the farm, causing suspicion. At this time, Chen then spoke to the students, saying that the students in Hunan were driven by people, so they advocated opposing him (Zhang Nong is from Hunan). He then proposed to the president that the horticultural area be separated from the farm and requested the resignation of Zhang Nong. Now that Zhang Chen is cooperating, the slogan of Hunan students being driven by people is no longer suitable for opposing Li Lianggong. Therefore, the expulsion of Chen by the students of the Horticulture Department has changed to Li Lianggong's presiding. The humble handwriting of arbitrarily accusing the student's claims of being instigated by one party to cope with private struggles, is there anything more than this in the world? (2) The expulsion of Fang Wu from the Agronomy and Chemistry Department also has its own bright and upright motives, not only because they opposed the hiring of a professor of soil science, but also because the motives of the two gentlemen Fang Wu were not pure, and the handwriting was even more despicable. They only used personal feelings to exclude dissidents and jointly wrote to the president to threaten their resignation, deceiving the students and disregarding the public interest. There is nothing more than this (to be continued)

West Qing Basketball Game Report Yesterday 102

Team Wins Rowing...32 to 22 Tong Wen Wins Nan Feng...24 to 17

The West Qing Basketball Association only held two Group B matches last night, starting at 7:50 PM. The two teams were evenly matched and competed fiercely, greatly exciting the audience. However, the performance was not yet perfect. The results were: (1) Team wins Rowing 32 to 22, (2) Tong Wen wins Nan Feng 24 to 17. There were no games tonight. Yesterday's battle report is as follows:

Team Wins Rowing

Rowing opened the scoring first, but the Team later took the lead, with a fairly good offensive strategy, once leading 16 to 2. They then scored 20 points. The four Rowing team players, Na Xian, successfully made two free throws, scoring four points. The first half ended with the Team leading 23 to 8. In the second half, Rowing launched a strong counterattack, scoring repeatedly and gaining momentum. The Team was on the verge of collapse, making the score 23 to 18 and 24 to 20. Although the Team was still leading by four or five points, they were in a precarious situation. They then rallied their spirits and persevered. Hu Zhikang and Yu Zhong successively scored, resulting in the Team winning the Rowing team 32 to 22. Referee: Wan Fu. The scores are as follows:
