Car Without License Plate Speeding on Dunxin Road 178

The Police Officer Ordered to Stop, but the Order Ignored. Both Sides Opened Fire, but No One Was Hit. Around 7 PM last night, a car without a license plate and no lights was speeding on Dunxin Road in western Shanghai. Its behavior was very suspicious. The police officer on duty saw it and ordered it to stop for inspection. However, the driver ignored the order and continued to drive forward. Suddenly, a gunshot was heard from the car. The officer drew his gun and fired back. Neither side was hit. The car eventually escaped. Whether the car was involved in kidnapping or other illegal activities remains to be investigated.

Receipt for Tobacco License Exempt from Stamp Duty 179

Error by Inspector. The Shanghai Tobacco Exchange Association sent a letter to the North and South City Offices regarding the exemption of stamp duty for temporary receipts for licenses. The letter stated: To Whom It May Concern: Regarding the case of the temporary receipts for tobacco licenses temporarily received by members of the association from the Jiangxi Second District Tobacco License Tax Collection Office being exempt from stamp duty, this association previously received a letter from Xiangcheng, a member company forwarded by the South City Office, requesting negotiation, which has been strongly argued. On the 15th of this month, we received a reply from the Jiangsu Shangbao Stamp Duty Bureau, stating that they have approved the association's letter stating that a member company, Xiangcheng, reported that a temporary receipt for a tobacco license was found by an inspector from the Shangbao Stamp Duty Bureau to have no stamp duty affixed and that the receipt was taken to the bureau for verification and return. The bureau considered that the temporary receipt was issued by the Tobacco and Alcohol License Collection Office for exchanging for a formal license and was not a deliberate omission of stamp duty. The inspector may have misunderstood and should be investigated and exempted, and the receipt should be returned. The bureau has already informed the bureau that this is not a formal tobacco and alcohol license, but a temporary receipt for applying for a license, and it is not a item to be affixed with stamp duty. The bureau has instructed the inspector to return it to the company on the same day to facilitate business, and has instructed all inspectors to be informed. In the future, this type of receipt will be exempt from investigation and deduction. If other merchants have similar receipts that have been mistakenly taken by inspectors to the bureau, they will be investigated and returned at any time after verification. The bureau's approval letter has been forwarded, and we hope that you will check and inquire with Xiangcheng whether the receipt has been returned to clarify the facts. On the same day, the bureau received a letter from your office requesting that members of the Nine Acres Land Company, Defeng, etc., have also experienced this situation and requesting further negotiation. Upon investigation, the inspectors clearly violated the bureau's orders and attempted to extort money. Except for the Dongjiadu Wanchang license, which was deducted due to negligence and omission of stamp duty, which should be handled separately, we will first forward the original letter from the bureau to all fellow tradesmen for response. Please check and handle it and, according to the items opened in the bureau's letter, contact the relevant offices to quickly negotiate the return of the deducted temporary receipts to clarify the original case and avoid disputes. In the meantime, the handling situation should still be reported at any time as it is necessary.

County Finance Bureau Collects Long-Term Registration Tax 180

Wang, the director of the Shanghai County Finance Bureau, found that the long-term registration tax was due. Therefore, he opened the list of more than 400 tax payers and issued them to the bailiff Yin Fengxiang for separate collection. It is limited to the end of the lunar year.

County Training Department's Recent Work 181

The Training Department of the Shanghai County Party Affairs Reorganization Committee has been sparing no effort in guiding the reorganization of various people's organizations in the county. It is reported that the organizations that have been initiated and reorganized in the county include the Minhang Chamber of Commerce, as well as the same-trade guilds of coolie clothing, Huami (a type of rice), and Nanhuo (goods from southern China). The Shanghai County Medical and Pharmaceutical Association, the student self-governing associations of county-run junior high schools and rural normal schools, and chambers of commerce in Beiqiao, Maqiao, and other places have all been investigated and approved by the department, and licenses have been issued. Zhou Bangjian, Lü Juefei, and others have been appointed as organizational instructors for the respective organizations. Starting from the 14th of this month, Department Head Han Rongling and staff member Zhou Bangjian personally went to various townships to investigate and provide guidance on the organization of various groups, and to explain the doubts about the newly promulgated regulations. They only returned to the committee last night. It is learned that although the department has repeatedly postponed the general registration of party ideology teachers in the county, the number of reporters coming to the department to register is still small. During this inspection of mass organizations, the department brought various registration forms to the schools for detailed investigation, and also conveniently inspected the implementation of party ideology education at all levels of the police. It is reported that the department plans to conduct an examination of party ideology education in the county together with the County Education Bureau and conduct single-level school party ideology tests in the near future.

Niu Huisheng Requests to Avoid Abolishing the Ministry of Health 182

Telegram from the Chinese Medical Association to President Song requesting: News from Nanjing Executive Yuan Acting President Song Yun reported that the Fourth Plenary Session's proposal to abolish the Ministry of Health and merge it into the Ministry of Interior has caused concern. Now that the domestic war has ended and construction is underway, health is of utmost importance. Moreover, the League of Nations has sent personnel to investigate China's health and has promised to do its best to assist in the design of the Ministry of Health. A dedicated department is necessary to take full responsibility. I respectfully request that Your Excellency strive to avoid the merger at the conference to comfort the people's hopes. Niu Huisheng, Chairman of the Chinese Medical Association, kowtows.

Jiang Dingwen Recovers and is Discharged from Hospital 184

General Jiang Dingwen came to Shanghai for medical treatment a few days ago due to excessive fatigue from fighting on the front lines, with coughing and discomfort. After arriving in Shanghai, he was introduced by a friend to the Chinese Lung Hospital, where he was carefully diagnosed by Dr. Wang Qizhang, a lung specialist and director of the hospital. He learned that although his lungs had been injured, it was not tuberculosis. The coughing was caused by a cold and inflammation of the trachea and bronchi. He can recover after resting for a few days. It is reported that he has fully recovered and been discharged from the hospital and is preparing to enter the capital.

Planning to Establish Kangjian Hospital 185

The Chinese Kangjian Association at 619 Nanjing Road was initiated by Xiong Shihui, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Du Yuesheng, Wang Tingsong, Yuan Ludeng, Zhao Jinqing, Diao Xinde, Yu Yunxiu, Gu Yuqi, Zhong Tingxing, Wang Qizhang, Zeng Liqun, and more than 40 others. The purpose of the association is to guide hygiene, provide medical advice, and promote the happiness of people's health. All undertakings related to the health needs of life will be carried out in turn. It is reported that the association believes that there are very few hospitals in Shanghai run by Chinese people with perfect equipment. Therefore, Gu Yuqi and Zeng Liqun, the medical directors of the association, are looking for a place to open a Kangjian Hospital. It is said that X-ray machines, radium ampoules, and various important electrical surgery equipment have all been ordered.

Wu Tiemei Opens Practice with Great Success 186

Wu Tiemei graduated from Tongji University and went to the University of Berlin in Germany to specialize in pediatrics. He then served as a doctor at the Freiburg University Pediatric Hospital for two years and obtained the highest grade medical doctorate degree. He has recently returned to China and set up a clinic at 182 Weihaiwei Road, Huaji Road, and the west end of Moore Road in this port. The practice opened on the 16th of this month. On that day, people from all walks of life went to congratulate him in an endless stream, and those who came to seek medical treatment were even more numerous.

Guangxuehui, located at the intersection of North Sichuan Road and Le'an Road, is one of the earliest institutions for communicating Chinese and Western cultures. The books it has published are numerous, and it has made outstanding achievements in Chinese cultural construction over the years. All the talents are contemporary masters, and the work in recent years has become increasingly vigorous. The original venue has become insufficient, so a seven-story building has been built and is currently under construction and will soon be completed. The association is scheduled to hold an open annual meeting at 4:15 this afternoon to report on the past situation of this session and future expansion plans. All sectors are welcome to come and participate, and refreshments will be provided to the guests. Dr. Li Denghui, President of Fudan University, and Dr. Ge Lan will all give important speeches.

Weather Report 190

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather is sunny and there is fog in the Yangtze River Basin and the coastal areas here. The Taiwan Strait has varying southeasterly to southwesterly winds. Liaodong has a cyclone due to a low pressure area passing through the area. There is also a low pressure area in southwestern China. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this port was 68.4 and the lowest was 45.3. On the same day of the previous year, the highest was 51.8 and the lowest was 30.2.

Qing Yi Se Restaurant at the intersection of Third Malu and Zhejiang Road declares that this restaurant is striving to improve Cantonese dishes and foods to ensure cleanliness, hygiene, affordable prices, and excellent service for both full-course meals and individual snacks. It is guaranteed to satisfy customers. This restaurant offers special economic lunches and dinners every day for individuals or groups of two people from all walks of life. Each meal costs five jiao, with hot stir-fries, cold appetizers, and soup served once each. Customers can choose from a specified menu, so it is quite popular among all walks of life. In addition, the restaurant's own Guangdong five-spice hygienic fermented bean curd and chili fermented bean curd are selling extremely well. Yesterday, more than 500 pots were delivered, and the prices remain the same: large pots are six jiao each, and small pots are 25 cents each. At this time of rising prices, this restaurant can make such sacrifices, which is truly rare. People from all walks of life are welcome to try it.

Automobile News

Special Article

Shanghai's Latest Automobile Statistics 197

— Pei Gan

Optimistic Outlook, Daily Improvements

After the sweltering heat of August, Shanghai's commerce gradually improved. In mid-September, the situation in various industries was better. As October arrived, the number of people inquiring about automobiles increased daily, and sales also improved daily. In particular, the development of the automobile industry by the Chinese people is the greatest. Automobile dealers in Shanghai have seen increasing sales and orders. From now until Christmas, there is reason to be optimistic. The number of automobiles registered in the autumn increased by 408, which shows that the business is still good. What is even more special is that many automobiles have been sold to the interior. For example, one brand of automobile is an excellent example of high-end automobiles. There are not many in the Shanghai area, but the dealer of this car said that more than 40 units were sold in mid-September, and there will be more transactions in the future.

Two automobile dealers also said that the demand for used cars in the market exceeds the supply. Once this ends, the outlet for new cars will inevitably be better. A dealer of Continental automobiles said that he has 40 new models of automobiles that have already been shipped to Shanghai and are on the way. Another batch of similar numbers is also planned to be shipped soon. As for the three types of American-made automobiles, Buick, Chrysler, and Studebaker, with eight cylinders, they have been on display in Shanghai for several weeks. Among them, the new Studebaker Free Wheel is especially attracting attention. With Shanghai's wealth, the status of multi-cylinder automobiles will naturally increase daily. Judging from the attached table, the number of automobile sales has not increased significantly, but the number of Riley, Wolseley, Morris, Whippet, and Willis is particularly high. Soon these companies will make further announcements. The number of automobile registrations in the third quarter of this year increased by 408 compared to the same period last year. It is particularly important to note that Shanghai automobile dealers not only operate in Shanghai, but also sell automobiles to Nanjing, Hangzhou, and even Hankou. The number of passenger cars increased by 101 in the Public Concession and 111 in the French Concession. As for the number of freight cars increased, the number of registrations in both the Public Concession and the French Concession on October 1 was 111 more than on July 1. The rest is the increase in motorcycles.

American-made automobiles still maintain their superior position. Although European-made automobiles have acceleration boosters and strive to compete in terms of price, they are still not very helpful. Among the 23 brands, 16 of those with more than 100 cars are made in the United States, four are from the United Kingdom, two are from France, one is from Italy, and one is a Feixiatuo. If we look at each automobile separately, Buick, which has been a leader for many years, still ranks first. The number of more than 1,000 cars is unprecedented in the history of Shanghai automobiles. There are currently 1,004 Buicks. Ford, a long-established automobile, ranks second, with the number of cars increasing every quarter. Currently, there are 940. Including trucks, there are a total of 1,652 Ford automobiles in the Shanghai Concession. This number is comparable to the number of Fords in American cities with similar populations to Shanghai. The combined sales of Chevrolet automobiles rank second, while the number of automobiles ranks third. There are a total of 961 Chevrolet automobiles and trucks in Shanghai. Among the automobiles manufactured in the United Kingdom, Morris Riley is the most numerous, with 526 units. Feixiatuo ranks second among Continental-made automobiles, with 505 units. Citroen and Austin rank third and fourth. Studebaker ranks above these two. See the table below for details.

Note (1) Public Automobile

Automobiles of Twenty-Six Years Ago 198

— Ding Zuze

The two attached photos are of the earliest products of the British Rolls-Royce automobile factory, dating back to 1904, twenty-one years ago. One of these two automobiles has a two-cylinder engine, and the other has a four-cylinder engine. Both were displayed at the Paris Motor Show and were considered the most beautiful automobiles of their time. One of them continuously traveled 220 miles in a single day without any difficulties. The Rolls-Royce automobile factory is the most famous high-end automobile manufacturer in England, producing extremely exquisite products, but only manufacturing the machinery and not the car body. The selling price is very high, with each set of machinery costing over 10,000 yuan.

Characteristics of Goodyear Aviation Tires 199

— Yun

How magnificent is the aviation industry! The development of transportation, the dissemination of news, the infusion of culture, the conduct of military affairs, and all other issues concerning national economy and people's livelihood mostly benefit from it directly or indirectly. Because of this, the aviation industry is increasingly valued by the world, and the issue of aviation safety is becoming increasingly important and urgently needs to be resolved by the world. In recent times, the efforts of various countries to promote the aviation industry and the exhaustive research and improvements by major manufacturers to enhance aviation safety all stem from a deep understanding of its significant importance, compelling them to spare no effort to continuously improve and achieve perfection.

The invention of Goodyear aviation tires is another new method to promote aviation safety and another great success of the company. Goodyear Rubber Company is one of the world's largest rubber factories, renowned globally for its robust strength, excellent products, magnificent scale, and comprehensive equipment. The company's innovative plans and numerous initiatives are particularly astonishing and admired by the world. This time, the company has focused its efforts on enhancing aviation safety, devoting its attention to meticulous research and development, ultimately leading to the invention of this new tire. Its structure, construction, and design are fundamentally innovative. Its functional characteristics aim to make aircraft takeoffs and landings safer. Its naming as the Goodyear aviation tire is due to the direct mounting of a full-volume pneumatic tire core onto the wheel hub. Thus, the rim, spokes, and wheel can all be eliminated. This combines the functions of both tire and wheel. Who would say its name is inappropriate?

The features of the tire-wheel are numerous, the most prominent being the valuable auxiliary shock absorber that can be eliminated, naturally increasing the load-carrying capacity. Landings are exceptionally stable, and the traction is particularly strong. Even when encountering ice, snow, or mud, the operation is very natural and has absolutely no impact on stability. Therefore, the usual ground equipment is not necessary here. When landing in windy conditions, it is even safer. Not only that, the aviation tire-wheel has a larger air capacity with the lowest pressure, so it can handle heavy loads under normal usage conditions. This has been verified through various tests. The tire core is placed on a specially made wheel hub. The internally expanding brake wheel can be installed or not, as desired, which is the same as the standard design. When an aircraft is equipped with this new type of aviation tire-wheel, landing is smooth and comfortable, with no jarring, and passengers can hardly discern when the aircraft touches the ground. Thus, the life of the aircraft can be extended. What is particularly noteworthy is that an aircraft equipped with aviation tire-wheels takes off more easily and requires less effort than one equipped with high-pressure tires. This is because it can still maintain contact with the ground through the tire's force when ascending two to five inches. Therefore, all obstacles on the ground are fully absorbed by the tire itself, and the aircraft's progress is not affected in the slightest. With these various advantages, the brisk sales of Goodyear aviation tire-wheels are undoubtedly predictable.

The various parts of the aircraft frame are free from the danger of damage or breakage. The reason why this type of tire-wheel can clearly absorb shocks and avoid bouncing is because of its low pressure and large air capacity. Even if there are shocks, they are dissipated in its larger air capacity. Furthermore, the cross-sectional diameter of the tire-wheel is particularly long compared to its height, so it naturally has the effect of a flat or webbed foot when landing, and the fuselage touching the ground or accumulated snow is also safer and without danger. High-pressure tires, on the other hand, may be prone to impact and other problems.

Buick Construction (Continued) 200

— Ji Ren

Increasingly Solid

Buick cars have gained the trust of the world because of their solid construction. Buick is a sturdy and durable car that provides reliable long-term service. The new 1931 Buick is even more capable of handling difficult tasks. Buick engineers are unwilling to reduce the car's weight easily, focusing on delivering sufficient power. The new chassis matches the new straight-eight-cylinder engine. All the major features of this year's new car, such as the sealed chassis, the entire powertrain, the driveshaft, and the pressed steel frame, are still preserved. The road handling of cars without a chassis has improved. The car body is solid and vibration-free, the chassis is stable, and the ride is comfortable. The chassis and body are made as one and have been tested on thousands of miles of rough roads. The frame is particularly sturdy, with a central heavy cross member. The size and strength of other cross members have also been increased. Heavy cross members are only found on expensive cars.

Talks on Road Administration in Beijing and Shanghai 202

— Wu Fei

Among the road administration issues nationwide, Shanghai ranks first, followed by Nanjing. Since Shanghai became a treaty port through the Sino-British Treaty, the concession areas have been gradually developed. The widening of roads, the solidity of roadbeds, the acquisition of houses, and the traffic of vehicles have a history of over eighty years and are still progressing daily. Even in the Chinese areas of Zhabei and Nanshi, active efforts are being made without reservation. Moreover, since the success of the Northern Expedition and the change to a special municipality, even more attention has been paid to road construction, such as the reconstruction of the Dongmen street with asphalt pavement, attention to sidewalks, and the return of vehicles from Ximen. In the three years since then, the achievements have been no less than those of the concessions. As for Nanjing, it is not so. The narrow and dilapidated streets, the obstructed and uneven road surfaces, the uneven heights of houses, and the muddy and slippery conditions after rain are undeniable. However, since the establishment of the National Government in Nanjing as the capital of China and a model city, the above-mentioned undesirable urban appearances should naturally be actively improved. Among them, Zhongshan Avenue directly reaches Sun Yat-sen Mausoleum and various road traffic is expected to be unified. Although it is not enough to compare with Shanghai, the model area is observed by both Chinese and foreigners, and it relies on the attention of the municipal authorities. How should the uneven road surfaces be made smooth? How should the narrow streets be widened? How should the inconvenient traffic be made rapid? How should the accidents caused by vehicles be reduced? It can be established as a rule for other places to follow and imitate. The issues of main roads, roadbed construction, selection of road construction materials, land acquisition and compensation, traffic signals, streetcars, and buses in Beijing and Shanghai are discussed separately below, with the intention of assisting others.

Main Roads in the City Whether the traffic in a city is developed depends on the prior determination of the main roads. Shanghai and Nanjing have successively measured and prepared detailed maps of the main roads in the city. The Shanghai concessions and the Public Works Department have accurate maps of the main roads in the city. The navigation of ports and the widening of streets are all detailed in advance and announced to the public. Citizens can formulate their own plans in accordance with the plans of the Public Works Department without hindering the city's plan to freely construct houses. If the main road is too narrow, the development of the city cannot meet the needs of traffic. If the main road is too wide, the waste of land is also very regrettable. Both Beijing and Shanghai have taken note of the concessions'

Page 27

determination of main road plans and have prepared detailed maps of the main roads in the city for public access.

Roadbed Construction If the roadbed is strong, heavy vehicles can travel. If the roadbed is weak, the road surface is easily damaged. Therefore, the Shanghai concessions' Public Works Department builds very thick roadbeds on all roads, with ten shichen or more being the most common. Even if there are many vehicles or many heavy vehicles, the road surface will not be damaged. Except for the existing roads, all newly built roads in Shanghai are also ten shichen or more. Zhongshan Road in Nanjing is also around ten shichen. The roadbed stones in both Beijing and Shanghai are generally large stone blocks, so even with many vehicles and frequent heavy vehicles, they can bear the weight. In areas where commerce and industry are developed, there are more heavy vehicles than elsewhere, and the roadbeds should be thickened accordingly. In administrative and residential areas, where there are fewer heavy vehicles, the roadbeds may be slightly thinner.

Selection of Materials The selection of road construction materials is also an important project, and asphalt roads are the most important. Asphalt roads are recognized as the most suitable road construction material in cities around the world. The Shanghai concessions have gradually converted stone roads to asphalt pavement. Although construction takes time and is more expensive, asphalt pavement is smooth and easy to clean, saving maintenance costs. Therefore, all new roads in Beijing and Shanghai are built with asphalt as the standard. Existing roads are also gradually repaired and repaved with asphalt. However, asphalt is not produced in China and must be purchased from overseas, increasing costs. It is said that the Kaiyuan Coal Mine Company manufactures a type of paving brick specifically for road construction. It is unknown whether this type of paving brick is suitable and is also a question for research. However, for the sake of reclaiming rights, it may be adopted and tested.

Land Acquisition and Compensation Providing reasonable land prices for land requisitioned is a fair method. In Shanghai, in addition to relocation expenses, land prices are paid in accordance with the Land Requisition Law, but at the same time, a road construction fee is levied based on the unearned increment in value. It is said that the construction cost of Zhongshan Road in Beijing is about 700,000 yuan, while demolition and land costs require tens of thousands of yuan. Therefore, land should be acquired with reasonable compensation, and at the same time, a road construction fee should be levied so that the rights and obligations of citizens are fair. It is said that Hangzhou, Hankou, and Guangzhou are following the same methods as Beijing and Shanghai.

Traffic Signals Traffic signals must have red and green lights. Red indicates stop, and green indicates go. This is a common traffic device used in cities around the world to direct vehicles and pedestrians. In Shanghai, where the population is increasing and traffic is complex, many of these traffic signals have been added. The Public Concession installed these lights first, and they were quite convenient. The French Concession also followed suit. This is nothing more than to reduce vehicle accidents. Vehicle accidents are unavoidable, but these lights reduce them slightly. However, they are only useful at intersections and three-way junctions on checkerboard-style streets. They are not necessary on winding streets. Therefore, although the Shanghai Municipal Government has been established for three years, it has installed few of these signal lights because the roads are mostly winding. After the construction of Zhongshan Road in Nanjing, traffic is concentrated on this road, and the municipal authorities have also installed these signal lights to ensure traffic safety. However, they are made of Chinese materials, and the style and candlepower are very weak, which is a shortcoming.

Streetcars and Automobiles Streetcars require tracks and overhead wires. Trackless streetcars have wires but no tracks. Buses do not require tracks or wires. The auto repair shops can be large or small. Therefore, the capital for streetcars must be strong and the scale must be large. Starting a bus company does not require much funding. When changes to routes are needed, a simple announcement is sufficient. The Shanghai concessions and urban areas have both streetcars and buses. Nanjing has long established a bus company, and streetcars are still being planned. However, the materials for streetcars must be purchased from Europe and the United States, and the equipment is very complex. Operating buses is easy, but the gasoline must be supplied by foreign countries, and the outflow of money is unbearable. In addition to the two concessions, the Shanghai Municipal Government has a Chinese-owned streetcar company operating on Zhonghua Road, Minguo Road, Gaochangmiao, and the Shiliupu Road. There is also the Hu-Min-Nan Tuo Bus Company operating on the Hu-Nan to Minhang line and the Hu-Nan Bus Company operating on the Nanshi and Zhabei lines. However, in recent years, the exchange rate has soared, and the price of automobiles has suddenly increased. It is proposed to increase fares to compensate for the losses. However, with the precedent of streetcars, the first increase in business was affected. I believe that Shanxi's oil wells are very rich and should be developed to supply domestic bus operators and reclaim rights.

All of the above are the most important aspects of road administration in Beijing and Shanghai. In short, our country has rarely paid attention to road administration. Since the establishment of the Shanghai concessions, people in our country have begun to realize that road administration is closely related to culture and transportation. Therefore, in recent years, cities and towns have built roads to facilitate automobile traffic and speed up travel. However, road administration issues are not easy to discuss. Our country has few scientific inventions, and industry is not developed. Not to mention that asphalt is imported, streetcar motors are purchased from abroad, and our country merely calls for building roads to facilitate transportation, unknowingly creating more profit opportunities and sales outlets for foreigners. How can we not be saddened when we think of this? Therefore, although I describe the road administration in Beijing and Shanghai as a reference for other places, I hope that: 1. Automobile manufacturing plants can be established in the country; 2. Oil wells in Shanxi Province can be developed; 3. Science can be studied in detail to manufacture streetcar motors; 4. Other suitable road construction materials besides asphalt can be found. There must be those who sympathize with this statement.

— Klao

Hudson automobiles have achieved results year after year. This year, the Polish Championship was won for the 19th time. The World's Longest Automobile Road 205

Running Directly Through North and South America - 15,000 Miles Long

According to news recently received from the United States, the California Automobile Association has decided to build the Inter-American Highway. All implementation methods are currently in place. The United States, its various states, North America's Alaska, and South America's Argentina are cooperating to connect North and South America. Once this road is completed, it will be the world's longest automobile road. The road will pass through California, Oregon, Washington, British Columbia, Burns, and South to Mexico and Central America along the Pacific coast and enter South America. The length of the route is rare and can be considered the world's longest automobile road. Since this news came out, governments in North and South America have been happy to support the early completion of this road. The border between British Columbia and Alaska is being planned. According to news from the United States, an office will be set up in Panama to connect various provinces and districts in Central America, measure routes, and discuss everything. This will be very convenient for the implementation. In the current situation, not only the United States, Canada, Mexico, and Central America are working hard, but also the government of the Republic of Argentina at the southern tip of South America is also striving to promote the implementation. According to news from official circles, the Argentine government has decided to first build a road across the Andes Mountains from Buenos Aires to Santiago, Chile, to Santiago, Chile, which is the center of the South American automobile road. This plateau road will be able to pass directly along the Pacific coast to Alaska and the provinces of North America, and the west coast of South America will also be able to reach Chile directly. Therefore, once this road is completed, the convenience of transportation between North and South America will be self-evident.

Amid these preparations, the US government has decided to allocate 50,000 gold yuan to measure the routes in various provinces in Central America. The Inter-American Highway Committee, which convened a meeting in Panama in mid-October last year, has been appointed by the US government to study the route, and the US Construction Committee will assist in all aspects of the measurement. The countries where the measurement is carried out must provide appropriate assistance to facilitate the process. Countries such as Costa Rica, Nicaragua, Guatemala, El Salvador, and Panama have formally expressed their willingness to assist in all aspects. When the Inter-American Highway is built in places where there are no roads, new roads must be built. Narrow roads in northern Canada and Alaska that can only be used by pack animals must be widened and rebuilt.

Page 28

There are two automobile groups in California that are cooperating: the California Automobile Association and the Southern California Automobile Club. British Columbia has good roads that can be extended to reach Canada, such as Revelstoke, Hope, and Fernie. During this road construction, officials from various countries and important figures in the automotive industry have met several times. The Yukon Territory of British Columbia, which is the only way for international automobiles, is also the plateau road along the Pacific coast. Four hundred miles will be built first, and construction will begin soon. Expedition members also held a formal meeting in Canada to decide on implementation methods to connect the routes in California, Oregon, and Washington. In fact, Alaska is almost an island nation, because there is no road for domestic transportation. In addition to steamships and transportation with the United States, automobiles cannot reach it. Once the Inter-American Highway is completed, all parts of the far north will be accessible, and Alaska will be especially convenient. The road is 15,000 miles long, starting from Fairbanks, Alaska in the north and reaching Santiago, Chile in the south. The length of the entire road is rare. We cannot help but regard it as a dream. However, Mexico, California, and other places have already started measuring, and the year of completion is not far away. We can wait and see.
